## Purpose

This file is the authoritative final-draft version of `f075v`.

`f75v` is a Book III bath page. SCALE TRANSITION — combines small purification batches into production-scale reservoir. Complex multi-level bath system with TWO SCALES of pools: small upper microchannels (approximately 10\) feeding into a larger lower reservoir containing approximately 19 nymph figures. Visible bridge connections between... A hierarchical flow controller: 10 microchannels feed a larger 19-body reservoir, with explicit bridge logic ensuring the global state stays coherent while moving between scales.

### Geometry

- `K.1`
  Equation:

  \[\gamma_{\mathrm{K_1}}^+ = G_{\mathrm{K_1}}(\gamma_{\mathrm{K_1}}^-)\]

  Variable legend: `gamma` is the route through the folio manifold.
  Reading: opaque operator line.
  Confidence: strong

### Game Theory

- `K.1`
  Equation:

  \[y_{\mathrm{K_1}}^+ = \operatorname*{argmin}_{y \in \Delta(\mathcal{A})}\{R_{\mathrm{K_1}}(y) + \lambda_{\mathrm{K_1}} C(y, y_{\mathrm{K_1}}^-)\}\]

  Variable legend: `y` is the strategy distribution; `R_line` is risk and `C` the control-cost.
  Reading: opaque operator line.
  Confidence: strong

## Direct Operational Meaning

A hierarchical flow controller: 10 microchannels feed a larger 19-body reservoir, with explicit bridge logic ensuring the global state stays coherent while moving between scales. Process statistics: 94 circulation commands (qo-); 13 valve/clamp checkpoints (ckh/kch); 10 infusion-stabilize cycles (shedy); 4 completion markers (daiin); 4 salt/crystallization references (sal).

## Mathematical Extraction

Across the formal lenses, `f75v` behaves as a fixed-point purification page with N_qo=69, N_valve=5, and N_seal=1. The governing update is x_(n+1) = V(C(x_n)); stop when ||x_(n+1)-x_n|| <= eps, then publish y = S(x_*).

## Mythic Extraction

`f75v` is a bathhouse-laboratory chamber: descend through linked pools, purify by circulation, prove stability at the clamps, and only then carry the living fluid onward.

`A hierarchical flow controller: 10 microchannels feed a larger 19-body reservoir, with explicit bridge logic ensuring the global state stays coherent while moving between scales.`

### Imported Kernel Equations

\[\mathcal H := L^2(\widehat{\mathbb C}, \mu), \qquad \rho \in \mathcal T_1(\mathcal H), \qquad \rho \succeq 0, \qquad \mathrm{Tr}(\rho)=1\]

\[\mathcal H_{\mathrm{tot}} = \left(\bigoplus_r \mathcal H_r\right) \oplus \left(\bigoplus_e \mathcal H_{\Lambda_e}\right) \oplus \mathcal H_{\mathrm{fail}}\]

\[x_{n+1}^{\mathrm{chem}} = K_n x_n^{\mathrm{chem}}, \qquad \mathbf{1}^T K_n = \mathbf{1}^T\]

\[g = \mathrm{Coll}(X), \qquad X = \mathrm{Expand}(g) \oplus r\]

\[\Phi_j^{(\lambda)} = T_\lambda^{-1} \circ \Phi_j^{(\mathrm{AQM})} \circ T_\lambda\]

### Typed State Machine

\[
\mathcal R_{f75v} = \{r_{charge}, r_{circulate}, r_{clamp}, r_{commit}, r_{seal}\}
\]
\[
\delta(r_{charge})=r_{circulate}, \qquad
\delta(r_{circulate})=r_{clamp}, \qquad
\delta(r_{clamp})=
\begin{cases}
r_{circulate} & \text{if } \Delta_n > 0 \\
r_{commit} & \text{if } \Delta_n = 0
\end{cases}
\]
\[
\delta(r_{commit})=
\begin{cases}
r_{seal} & \text{if } P_{salt} = 1 \\
r_{circulate} & \text{otherwise}
\end{cases}
\]
